focus_tree = {
	id = polish_focus
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 20
			tag = POL
		}
	}
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 6100 y = 3000 }

	focus = {
		id = POL_revitalize_government
		icon = Poland
		x = 20
		y = 0
		cost = 5

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus POL_revitalize_government"
			add_political_power = 120
		}

		ai_will_do = { factor = 50 }
	}

	focus = {
		id = POL_change_of_path
		icon = anti_democracy2
		x = 13
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = POL_revitalize_government
		cost = 5

		allow_branch = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = POL_stay_on_track
			}
		}

		prerequisite = { focus = POL_revitalize_government }
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = POL_stay_on_track }

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus POL_change_of_path"
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = POL_stay_on_track
		icon = support_democracy
		x = -10
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = POL_revitalize_government
		cost = 5

		allow_branch = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = POL_change_of_path
			}
		}

		prerequisite = { focus = POL_revitalize_government }

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY }

			}
		}

############################################################### New Communist Tree (XCezor) ###################################################################################

	focus = {
		id = POL_red_dream
		icon = soc_rev_blr
		x = -3
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = POL_change_of_path
		cost = 10

		allow_branch = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = POL_falanga
			}
		}
		allow_branch = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = POL_stay_on_track
			}
		}

		prerequisite = {
			focus = POL_change_of_path
		}

		mutually_exclusive = { focus = POL_falanga }

		search_filters = {
			FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL
			FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS
			FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus POL_red_dream"
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = POL_communism_uprising_again_activation
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 5 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.12 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.12 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.12 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes

				add_ideas = POL_economy_status1_idea
				add_ideas = POL_solidarity_strength1_idea
				add_ideas = POL_communism_domination1_idea

				add_political_power = 75
				custom_effect_tooltip = POL_leave_nato_warning_TT
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = POL_communism_domination5_idea
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 5 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.5 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 4 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.5 }
				set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.5 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 4 }
						change_ruling_party_effect = yes
						hidden_effect = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = communism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							set_popularities = {
								democratic = 0
								neutrality = 0
								fascism = 0
								communism = 100
							}
							NATO_leave = yes
						}
					}
					50 = {
						set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 5 }
						change_ruling_party_effect = yes
						hidden_effect = {
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = communism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							set_popularities = {
								democratic = 0
								neutrality = 0
								fascism = 0
								communism = 100
							}
							NATO_leave = yes
						}
					}
				}

				complete_national_focus = POL_fight_the_democracy
				complete_national_focus = POL_strike_the_government
				complete_national_focus = POL_negative_effects_of_privatization
				complete_national_focus = POL_antagonize_the_europe
			}

			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				add = 75
			}
		}
	}

			FOCUS_FILTER_INTERNAL_AFFAIRS
		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus POL_reduce_trade"
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = semi_consumption_economy }

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = semi_consumption_economy
					add_idea = consumption_economy
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = mixed_economy }

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = mixed_economy
					add_idea = consumption_economy
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = export_economy }

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = export_economy
					add_idea = consumption_economy
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = globalized_trade_economy }

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = globalized_trade_economy
					add_idea = consumption_economy
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
			change_international_bankers_opinion = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = { factor = 50 }
	}

				}
			}
		}
